    WHERE (((((((([o].[Active] = 1) AND ([a].[Active] = 1)) AND ([o1].[Active] = 1)) AND ([a0].[Active] = 1)) AND ([p].[Active] = 1)) AND ([p0].[Active] = 1)) AND ([p1].[Active] = 1)) AND ([p2].[Active] = 1)) AND ((([o].[OrderStatusId] = @__DEPOSITED_0) OR ([o].[OrderStatusId] = @__PURCHAED_1)) OR ([o].[OrderStatusId] = @__APPROVED_2))
    ORDER BY [o].[Id] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_3 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_4 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a1].[Username], [a1].[Password], [o2].[Description], [o2].[Id], [a1].[Id] AS [Id0], [o2].[OrderId]
    FROM [OrderAccount] AS [o2]
    INNER JOIN [AccountBuy] AS [a1] ON [o2].[AccountBuyId] = [a1].[Id]
    WHERE ([o2].[Active] = 1) AND ([a1].[Active] = 1)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[OrderId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a2].[Username], [a2].[Password], [o3].[Description], [o3].[Id], [a2].[Id] AS [Id0], [o3].[OrderId]
    FROM [OrderAccount] AS [o3]
    INNER JOIN [AccountBuy] AS [a2] ON [o3].[AccountBuyId] = [a2].[Id]
    WHERE ([o3].[Active] = 1) AND ([a2].[Active] = 1)
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[OrderId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id] DESC, [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t].[Id2], [t].[Id3], [t].[Id4], [t].[Id5], [t].[Id6], [t].[Id7], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [t1].[Id]
